5116                                                       vca_result);
5117       if (msg == NULL) {
5118         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5119         Exceptions::fthrow(
5120           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5121           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5122           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5123           this_klass->external_name(),
5124           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5125           super->external_name(),
5126           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5127           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5128           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5129       } else {
5130         // Add additional message content.
5131         Exceptions::fthrow(
5132           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5133           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5134           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5135           msg);
5136       }
5137     }
5138   }
5139 }
5140 
5141 
5142 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5143   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5144   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5145   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5146   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5147     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5148     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5149     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5150       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5151     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5152       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5153       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5154                                                       k,
5155                                                       vca_result);
5156       if (msg == NULL) {
5157         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == k->module());
5158         Exceptions::fthrow(
5159           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5160           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5161           "class %s cannot access its superinterface %s (%s%s%s)",
5162           this_klass->external_name(),
5163           k->external_name(),
5164           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(k) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5165           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5166           (same_module) ? "" : k->class_in_module_of_loader());
5167       } else {
5168         // Add additional message content.
5169         Exceptions::fthrow(
5170           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5171           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5172           "superinterface check failed: %s",
5173           msg);
5174       }
5175     }
5176   }
5177 }
5178 
5179 
5180 static void check_final_method_override(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5181   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5182   const Array<Method*>* const methods = this_klass->methods();
5183   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5184 
5185   // go thru each method and check if it overrides a final method
5186   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5187     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5188 
5189     // skip private, static, and <init> methods
5190     if ((!m->is_private() && !m->is_static()) &&
5191         (m->name() != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name())) {
5192 
5193       const Symbol* const name = m->name();
5194       const Symbol* const signature = m->signature();
5195       const Klass* k = this_klass->super();
5196       const Method* super_m = NULL;
5197       while (k != NULL) {
5198         // skip supers that don't have final methods.
5199         if (k->has_final_method()) {
5200           // lookup a matching method in the super class hierarchy
5201           super_m = InstanceKlass::cast(k)->lookup_method(name, signature);
5202           if (super_m == NULL) {
5203             break; // didn't find any match; get out
5204           }
5205 
5206           if (super_m->is_final() && !super_m->is_static() &&
5207               !super_m->access_flags().is_private()) {
5208             // matching method in super is final, and not static or private
5209             bool can_access = Reflection::verify_member_access(this_klass,
5210                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5211                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5212                                                                super_m->access_flags(),
5213                                                               false, false, CHECK);
5214             if (can_access) {
5215               // this class can access super final method and therefore override
5216               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5217               Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5218                                  vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5219                                  "class %s overrides final method %s.%s%s",
5220                                  this_klass->external_name(),
5221                                  super_m->method_holder()->external_name(),
5222                                  name->as_C_string(),
5223                                  signature->as_C_string()
5224                                  );
5225               return;
5226             }
5227           }
5228 
5229           // continue to look from super_m's holder's super.
5230           k = super_m->method_holder()->super();
5231           continue;
5232         }
5233 
5234         k = k->super();
5235       }
5236     }
5237   }
5238 }
5239 
5240 
5241 // assumes that this_klass is an interface
5242 static void check_illegal_static_method(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5243   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5244   assert(this_klass->is_interface(), "not an interface");
5245   const Array<Method*>* methods = this_klass->methods();
5246   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5247 
5248   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5249     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5250     // if m is static and not the init method, throw a verify error
5251     if ((m->is_static()) && (m->name() != vmSymbols::class_initializer_name())) {
5252       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5253       Exceptions::fthrow(
5254         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5255         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5256         "Illegal static method %s in interface %s",
5257         m->name()->as_C_string(),
5258         this_klass->external_name()
5259       );
5260       return;
5261     }
5262   }
5263 }
5264 
5265 // utility methods for format checking
5266 
5267 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_modifiers(jint flags, TRAPS) const {
5268   const bool is_module = (flags & JVM_ACC_MODULE) != 0;
5269   const bool is_inline_type = (flags & JVM_ACC_VALUE) != 0;
5270   assert(_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION || !is_module, "JVM_ACC_MODULE should not be set");
5271   assert(supports_inline_types() || !is_inline_type, "JVM_ACC_VALUE should not be set");
5272   if (is_module) {
5273     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5274     Exceptions::fthrow(
5275       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5276       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
5277       "%s is not a class because access_flag ACC_MODULE is set",
5278       _class_name->as_C_string());
5279     return;
5280   }
5281 
5282   if (is_inline_type && !EnableValhalla) {
5283     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5284     Exceptions::fthrow(
5285       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5286       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5287       "Class modifier ACC_VALUE in class %s requires option -XX:+EnableValhalla",
5288       _class_name->as_C_string()
5289     );
5290   }
5291 
5292   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5293 
5294   const bool is_interface  = (flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE)  != 0;
5295   const bool is_abstract   = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)   != 0;
5296   const bool is_final      = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)      != 0;
5297   const bool is_super      = (flags & JVM_ACC_SUPER)      != 0;
5298   const bool is_enum       = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)       != 0;
5299   const bool is_annotation = (flags & JVM_ACC_ANNOTATION) != 0;
5300   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5301   const bool major_gte_14  = _major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION;
5302 
5303   if ((is_abstract && is_final) ||
5304       (is_interface && !is_abstract) ||
5305       (is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && (is_super || is_enum)) ||
5306       (!is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && is_annotation) ||
5307       (is_inline_type && (is_interface || is_abstract || is_enum || !is_final))) {
5308     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5309     const char* class_note = "";
5310     if (is_inline_type)  class_note = " (an inline class)";
5311     Exceptions::fthrow(
5312       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5313       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5314       "Illegal class modifiers in class %s%s: 0x%X",
5315       _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags
5316     );
5317     return;
5318   }
5319 }
5320 
5321 static bool has_illegal_visibility(jint flags) {
5322   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5323   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5324   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5325 
5326   return ((is_public && is_protected) ||
5327           (is_public && is_private) ||
5328           (is_protected && is_private));
5329 }
5330 
5331 // A legal major_version.minor_version must be one of the following:
5332 //
5333 //  Major_version >= 45 and major_version < 56, any minor_version.
5334 //  Major_version >= 56 and major_version <= JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 0.
5335 //  Major_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 65535 and --enable-preview is present.
5336 //
5337 static void verify_class_version(u2 major, u2 minor, Symbol* class_name, TRAPS){
5338   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5339   const u2 max_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
5340   if (major < JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION) {
5341     Exceptions::fthrow(
5342       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5343       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5344       "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid major version",
5345       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5346     return;
5347   }
5348 
5349   if (major > max_version) {
5350     Exceptions::fthrow(
5351       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5352       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5353       "%s has been compiled by a more recent version of the Java Runtime (class file version %u.%u), "
5354       "this version of the Java Runtime only recognizes class file versions up to %u.0",
5355       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
5356     return;
5357   }
5358 
5359   if (major < JAVA_12_VERSION || minor == 0) {
5360     return;
5361   }
5362 
5363   if (minor == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION) {
5364     if (major != max_version) {
5365       Exceptions::fthrow(
5366         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5367         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5368         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with preview features that are unsupported. "
5369         "This version of the Java Runtime only recognizes preview features for class file version %u.%u",
5370         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION, JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION);
5371       return;
5372     }
5373 
5374     if (!Arguments::enable_preview()) {
5375       Exceptions::fthrow(
5376         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5377         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5378         "Preview features are not enabled for %s (class file version %u.%u). Try running with '--enable-preview'",
5379         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5380       return;
5381     }
5382 
5383   } else { // minor != JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION
5384     Exceptions::fthrow(
5385         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5386         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5387         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid non-zero minor version",
5388         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5389   }
5390 }
5391 
5392 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_modifiers(jint flags,
5393                                                    bool is_interface,
5394                                                    bool is_inline_type,
5395                                                    TRAPS) const {
5396   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5397 
5398   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5399   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5400   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5401   const bool is_static    = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)    != 0;
5402   const bool is_final     = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)     != 0;
5403   const bool is_volatile  = (flags & JVM_ACC_VOLATILE)  != 0;
5404   const bool is_transient = (flags & JVM_ACC_TRANSIENT) != 0;
5405   const bool is_enum      = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)      != 0;
5406   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5407 
5408   bool is_illegal = false;
5409 
5410   if (is_interface) {
5411     if (!is_public || !is_static || !is_final || is_private ||
5412         is_protected || is_volatile || is_transient ||
5413         (major_gte_1_5 && is_enum)) {
5414       is_illegal = true;
5415     }
5416   } else { // not interface
5417     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags) || (is_final && is_volatile)) {
5418       is_illegal = true;
5419     } else {
5420       if (is_inline_type && !is_static && !is_final) {
5421         is_illegal = true;
5422       }
5423     }
5424   }
5425 
5426   if (is_illegal) {
5427     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5428     Exceptions::fthrow(
5429       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5430       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5431       "Illegal field modifiers in class %s: 0x%X",
5432       _class_name->as_C_string(), flags);
5433     return;
5434   }
5435 }
5436 
5437 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_modifiers(jint flags,
5438                                                     bool is_interface,
5439                                                     bool is_inline_type,
5440                                                     const Symbol* name,
5441                                                     TRAPS) const {
5442   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5443 
5444   const bool is_public       = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)       != 0;
5445   const bool is_private      = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)      != 0;
5446   const bool is_static       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)       != 0;
5447   const bool is_final        = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)        != 0;
5448   const bool is_native       = (flags & JVM_ACC_NATIVE)       != 0;
5449   const bool is_abstract     = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)     != 0;
5450   const bool is_bridge       = (flags & JVM_ACC_BRIDGE)       != 0;
5451   const bool is_strict       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STRICT)       != 0;
5452   const bool is_synchronized = (flags & JVM_ACC_SYNCHRONIZED) != 0;
5453   const bool is_protected    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED)    != 0;
5454   const bool major_gte_1_5   = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5455   const bool major_gte_8     = _major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION;
5456   const bool is_initializer  = (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name());
5457 
5458   bool is_illegal = false;
5459 
5460   const char* class_note = "";
5461 
5462   if (is_interface) {
5463     if (major_gte_8) {
5464       // Class file version is JAVA_8_VERSION or later Methods of
5465       // interfaces may set any of the flags except ACC_PROTECTED,
5466       // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, and ACC_SYNCHRONIZED; they must
5467       // have exactly one of the ACC_PUBLIC or ACC_PRIVATE flags set.
5468       if ((is_public == is_private) || /* Only one of private and public should be true - XNOR */
5469           (is_native || is_protected || is_final || is_synchronized) ||
5470           // If a specific method of a class or interface has its
5471           // ACC_ABSTRACT flag set, it must not have any of its
5472           // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, ACC_PRIVATE, ACC_STATIC,
5473           // ACC_STRICT, or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED flags set.  No need to
5474           // check for ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED as
5475           // those flags are illegal irrespective of ACC_ABSTRACT being set or not.
5476           (is_abstract && (is_private || is_static || is_strict))) {
5477         is_illegal = true;
5478       }
5479     } else if (major_gte_1_5) {
5480       // Class file version in the interval [JAVA_1_5_VERSION, JAVA_8_VERSION)
5481       if (!is_public || is_private || is_protected || is_static || is_final ||
5482           is_synchronized || is_native || !is_abstract || is_strict) {
5483         is_illegal = true;
5484       }
5485     } else {
5486       // Class file version is pre-JAVA_1_5_VERSION
5487       if (!is_public || is_static || is_final || is_native || !is_abstract) {
5488         is_illegal = true;
5489       }
5490     }
5491   } else { // not interface
5492     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags)) {
5493       is_illegal = true;
5494     } else {
5495       if (is_initializer) {
5496         if (is_final || is_synchronized || is_native ||
5497             is_abstract || (major_gte_1_5 && is_bridge)) {
5498           is_illegal = true;
5499         }
5500         if (!is_static && !is_inline_type) {
5501           // OK, an object constructor in a regular class
5502         } else if (is_static && is_inline_type) {
5503           // OK, a static init factory in an inline class
5504         } else {
5505           // but no other combinations are allowed
5506           is_illegal = true;
5507           class_note = (is_inline_type ? " (an inline class)" : " (not an inline class)");
5508         }
5509       } else { // not initializer
5510         if (is_inline_type && is_synchronized && !is_static) {
5511           is_illegal = true;
5512           class_note = " (an inline class)";
5513         } else {
5514           if (is_abstract) {
5515             if ((is_final || is_native || is_private || is_static ||
5516                 (major_gte_1_5 && (is_synchronized || is_strict)))) {
5517               is_illegal = true;
5518             }
5519           }
5520         }
5521       }
5522     }
5523   }
5524 
5525   if (is_illegal) {
5526     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5527     Exceptions::fthrow(
5528       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5529       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5530       "Method %s in class %s%s has illegal modifiers: 0x%X",
5531       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags);
5532     return;
5533   }
5534 }
5535 
5536 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_utf8(const unsigned char* buffer,
5537                                         int length,
5538                                         TRAPS) const {
5539   assert(_need_verify, "only called when _need_verify is true");
5540   if (!UTF8::is_legal_utf8(buffer, length, _major_version <= 47)) {
5541     classfile_parse_error("Illegal UTF8 string in constant pool in class file %s", CHECK);
5542   }
5543 }
5544 
5545 // Unqualified names may not contain the characters '.', ';', '[', or '/'.
5546 // In class names, '/' separates unqualified names.  This is verified in this function also.
5547 // Method names also may not contain the characters '<' or '>', unless <init>
5548 // or <clinit>.  Note that method names may not be <init> or <clinit> in this
5549 // method.  Because these names have been checked as special cases before
5550 // calling this method in verify_legal_method_name.
5551 //
5552 // This method is also called from the modular system APIs in modules.cpp
5553 // to verify the validity of module and package names.
5554 bool ClassFileParser::verify_unqualified_name(const char* name,
5555                                               unsigned int length,
5556                                               int type) {
5557   if (length == 0) return false;  // Must have at least one char.
5558   for (const char* p = name; p != name + length; p++) {
5559     switch(*p) {
5560       case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT:
5561       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS:
5562       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5563         // do not permit '.', ';', or '['
5564         return false;
5565       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH:
5566         // check for '//' or leading or trailing '/' which are not legal
5567         // unqualified name must not be empty
5568         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalClass) {
5569           if (p == name || p+1 >= name+length ||
5570               *(p+1) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5571             return false;
5572           }
5573         } else {
5574           return false;   // do not permit '/' unless it's class name
5575         }
5576         break;
5577       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL:
5578       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDSPECIAL:
5579         // do not permit '<' or '>' in method names
5580         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalMethod) {
5581           return false;
5582         }
5583     }
5584   }
5585   return true;
5586 }
5587 
5588 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5589 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5590 // be taken as a fieldname. Allow '/' if slash_ok is true.
5591 // Return a pointer to just past the fieldname.
5592 // Return NULL if no fieldname at all was found, or in the case of slash_ok
5593 // being true, we saw consecutive slashes (meaning we were looking for a
5594 // qualified path but found something that was badly-formed).
5595 static const char* skip_over_field_name(const char* const name,
5596                                         bool slash_ok,
5597                                         unsigned int length) {
5598   const char* p;
5599   jboolean last_is_slash = false;
5600   jboolean not_first_ch = false;
5601 
5602   for (p = name; p != name + length; not_first_ch = true) {
5603     const char* old_p = p;
5604     jchar ch = *p;
5605     if (ch < 128) {
5606       p++;
5607       // quick check for ascii
5608       if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z') ||
5609         (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z') ||
5610         (ch == '_' || ch == '$') ||
5611         (not_first_ch && ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')) {
5612         last_is_slash = false;
5613         continue;
5614       }
5615       if (slash_ok && ch == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5616         if (last_is_slash) {
5617           return NULL;  // Don't permit consecutive slashes
5618         }
5619         last_is_slash = true;
5620         continue;
5621       }
5622     }
5623     else {
5624       jint unicode_ch;
5625       char* tmp_p = UTF8::next_character(p, &unicode_ch);
5626       p = tmp_p;
5627       last_is_slash = false;
5628       // Check if ch is Java identifier start or is Java identifier part
5629       // 4672820: call java.lang.Character methods directly without generating separate tables.
5630       EXCEPTION_MARK;
5631       // return value
5632       JavaValue result(T_BOOLEAN);
5633       // Set up the arguments to isJavaIdentifierStart or isJavaIdentifierPart
5634       JavaCallArguments args;
5635       args.push_int(unicode_ch);
5636 
5637       if (not_first_ch) {
5638         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierPart(char ch);
5639         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5640           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5641           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierPart_name(),
5642           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5643           &args,
5644           THREAD);
5645       } else {
5646         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierStart(char ch);
5647         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5648           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5649           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierStart_name(),
5650           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5651           &args,
5652           THREAD);
5653       }
5654       if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION) {
5655         CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION;
5656         return NULL;
5657       }
5658       if(result.get_jboolean()) {
5659         continue;
5660       }
5661     }
5662     return (not_first_ch) ? old_p : NULL;
5663   }
5664   return (not_first_ch) ? p : NULL;
5665 }
5666 
5667 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5668 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5669 // be taken as a field signature. Allow "void" if void_ok.
5670 // Return a pointer to just past the signature.
5671 // Return NULL if no legal signature is found.
5672 const char* ClassFileParser::skip_over_field_signature(const char* signature,
5673                                                        bool void_ok,
5674                                                        unsigned int length,
5675                                                        TRAPS) const {
5676   unsigned int array_dim = 0;
5677   while (length > 0) {
5678     switch (signature[0]) {
5679     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID: if (!void_ok) { return NULL; }
5680     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BOOLEAN:
5681     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BYTE:
5682     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CHAR:
5683     case JVM_SIGNATURE_SHORT:
5684     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INT:
5685     case JVM_SIGNATURE_FLOAT:
5686     case JVM_SIGNATURE_LONG:
5687     case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOUBLE:
5688       return signature + 1;
5689     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VALUETYPE:
5690       // Can't enable this check until JDK upgrades the bytecode generators
5691       // if (_major_version < CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS ) {
5692       //   classfile_parse_error("Class name contains illegal Q-signature "
5693       //                                    "in descriptor in class file %s",
5694       //                                    CHECK_0);
5695       // }
5696       // fall through
5697     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CLASS:
5698     {
5699       if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5700         // Skip over the class name if one is there
5701         const char* const p = skip_over_field_name(signature + 1, true, --length);
5702 
5703         // The next character better be a semicolon
5704         if (p && (p - signature) > 1 && p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS) {
5705           return p + 1;
5706         }
5707       }
5708       else {
5709         // Skip leading 'L' or 'Q' and ignore first appearance of ';'
5710         signature++;
5711         const char* c = (const char*) memchr(signature, JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS, length - 1);
5712         // Format check signature
5713         if (c != NULL) {
5714           int newlen = c - (char*) signature;
5715           bool legal = verify_unqualified_name(signature, newlen, LegalClass);
5716           if (!legal) {
5717             classfile_parse_error("Class name is empty or contains illegal character "
5718                                   "in descriptor in class file %s",
5719                                   CHECK_NULL);
5720             return NULL;
5721           }
5722           return signature + newlen + 1;
5723         }
5724       }
5725       return NULL;
5726     }
5727     case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5728       array_dim++;
5729       if (array_dim > 255) {
5730         // 4277370: array descriptor is valid only if it represents 255 or fewer dimensions.
5731         classfile_parse_error("Array type descriptor has more than 255 dimensions in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
5732       }
5733       // The rest of what's there better be a legal signature
5734       signature++;
5735       length--;
5736       void_ok = false;
5737       break;
5738     default:
5739       return NULL;
5740     }
5741   }
5742   return NULL;
5743 }
5744 
5745 // Checks if name is a legal class name.
5746 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5747   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5748 
5749   assert(name->refcount() > 0, "symbol must be kept alive");
5750   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5751   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5752   bool legal = false;
5753 
5754   if (length > 0) {
5755     const char* p;
5756     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY) {
5757       p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5758       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5759     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5760       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5761         p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, true, length);
5762         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5763       }
5764     } else if (_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS && bytes[length - 1] == ';' ) {
5765       // Support for L...; and Q...; descriptors
5766       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes + 1, length - 2, LegalClass);
5767     } else {
5768       // 4900761: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5769       // Class names may be drawn from the entire Unicode character set.
5770       // Identifiers between '/' must be unqualified names.
5771       // The utf8 string has been verified when parsing cpool entries.
5772       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalClass);
5773     }
5774   }
5775   if (!legal) {
5776     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5777     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5778     Exceptions::fthrow(
5779       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5780       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5781       "Illegal class name \"%.*s\" in class file %s", length, bytes,
5782       _class_name->as_C_string()
5783     );
5784     return;
5785   }
5786 }
5787 
5788 // Checks if name is a legal field name.
5789 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5790   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5791 
5792   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5793   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5794   bool legal = false;
5795 
5796   if (length > 0) {
5797     if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5798       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5799         const char* p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5800         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5801       }
5802     } else {
5803       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5804       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalField);
5805     }
5806   }
5807 
5808   if (!legal) {
5809     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5810     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5811     Exceptions::fthrow(
5812       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5813       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5814       "Illegal field name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5815       _class_name->as_C_string()
5816     );
5817     return;
5818   }
5819 }
5820 
5821 // Checks if name is a legal method name.
5822 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5823   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5824 
5825   assert(name != NULL, "method name is null");
5826   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5827   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5828   bool legal = false;
5829 
5830   if (length > 0) {
5831     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5832       if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() || name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
5833         legal = true;
5834       }
5835     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5836       const char* p;
5837       p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5838       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5839     } else {
5840       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5841       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalMethod);
5842     }
5843   }
5844 
5845   if (!legal) {
5846     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5847     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5848     Exceptions::fthrow(
5849       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5850       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5851       "Illegal method name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5852       _class_name->as_C_string()
5853     );
5854     return;
5855   }
5856 }
5857 
5858 
5859 // Checks if signature is a legal field signature.
5860 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_signature(const Symbol* name,
5861                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5862                                                    TRAPS) const {
5863   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5864 
5865   const char* const bytes = (const char* const)signature->bytes();
5866   const unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5867   const char* const p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5868 
5869   if (p == NULL || (p - bytes) != (int)length) {
5870     throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
5871   }
5872 }
5873 
5874 // Checks if signature is a legal method signature.
5875 // Returns number of parameters
5876 int ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_signature(const Symbol* name,
5877                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5878                                                    TRAPS) const {
5879   if (!_need_verify) {
5880     // make sure caller's args_size will be less than 0 even for non-static
5881     // method so it will be recomputed in compute_size_of_parameters().
5882     return -2;
5883   }
5884 
5885   // Class initializers cannot have args for class format version >= 51.
5886   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name() &&
5887       signature != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
5888       _major_version >= JAVA_7_VERSION) {
5889     throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5890     return 0;
5891   }
5892 
5893   unsigned int args_size = 0;
5894   const char* p = (const char*)signature->bytes();
5895   unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5896   const char* nextp;
5897 
5898   // The first character must be a '('
5899   if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_FUNC)) {
5900     length--;
5901     // Skip over legal field signatures
5902     nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5903     while ((length > 0) && (nextp != NULL)) {
5904       args_size++;
5905       if (p[0] == 'J' || p[0] == 'D') {
5906         args_size++;
5907       }
5908       length -= nextp - p;
5909       p = nextp;
5910       nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5911     }
5912     // The first non-signature thing better be a ')'
5913     if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDFUNC)) {
5914       length--;
5915       if (name->utf8_length() > 0 && name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5916         // All constructor methods must return void
5917         if ((length == 1) && (p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID)) {
5918           return args_size;
5919         }
5920         // All static init methods must return the current class
5921         if ((length >= 3) && (p[length-1] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS)
5922             && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
5923           nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5924           if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5925             // The actual class will be checked against current class
5926             // when the method is defined (see parse_method).
5927             // A reference to a static init with a bad return type
5928             // will load and verify OK, but will fail to link.
5929             return args_size;
5930           }
5931         }
5932         // The distinction between static factory methods and
5933         // constructors depends on the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier.
5934         // This distinction must be reflected in a void or non-void
5935         // return. For declared methods, the check is in parse_method.
5936       } else {
5937         // Now we better just have a return value
5938         nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5939         if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5940           return args_size;
5941         }
5942       }
5943     }
5944   }
5945   // Report error
5946   throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5947   return 0;
5948 }
5949 
5950 int ClassFileParser::static_field_size() const {
5951   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5952   return _field_info->_static_field_size;
5953 }

5955 int ClassFileParser::total_oop_map_count() const {
5956   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5957   return _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count;
5958 }
