5960 jint ClassFileParser::layout_size() const {
5961   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5962   return _field_info->_instance_size;
5963 }
5964 
5965 static void check_methods_for_intrinsics(const InstanceKlass* ik,
5966                                          const Array<Method*>* methods) {
5967   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
5968   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
5969 
5970   // Set up Method*::intrinsic_id as soon as we know the names of methods.
5971   // (We used to do this lazily, but now we query it in Rewriter,
5972   // which is eagerly done for every method, so we might as well do it now,
5973   // when everything is fresh in memory.)
5974   const vmSymbols::SID klass_id = Method::klass_id_for_intrinsics(ik);
5975 
5976   if (klass_id != vmSymbols::NO_SID) {
5977     for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
5978       Method* method = methods->at(j);
5979       method->init_intrinsic_id();
5980 
5981       if (CheckIntrinsics) {
5982         // Check if an intrinsic is defined for method 'method',
5983         // but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.
5984         if (method->intrinsic_id() != vmIntrinsics::_none &&
5985             !method->intrinsic_candidate()) {
5986               tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
5987               "but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.%s",
5988               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5989               NOT_DEBUG(" Method will not be inlined.") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5990             );
5991           tty->cr();
5992           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5993         }
5994         // Check is the method 'method' is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
5995         // but there is no intrinsic available for it.
5996         if (method->intrinsic_candidate() &&
5997           method->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none) {
5998             tty->print("Method [%s] is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate, "
5999               "but no compiler intrinsic is defined for the method.%s",
6000               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
6001               NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6002             );
6003           tty->cr();
6004           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6005         }
6006       }
6007     } // end for
6008 
6009 #ifdef ASSERT
6010     if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6011       // Check for orphan methods in the current class. A method m
6012       // of a class C is orphan if an intrinsic is defined for method m,
6013       // but class C does not declare m.
6014       // The check is potentially expensive, therefore it is available
6015       // only in debug builds.
6016 
6017       for (int id = vmIntrinsics::FIRST_ID; id < (int)vmIntrinsics::ID_LIMIT; ++id) {
6018         if (vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm == id) {
6019           // The _compiledLamdbdaForm intrinsic is a special marker for bytecode
6020           // generated for the JVM from a LambdaForm and therefore no method
6021           // is defined for it.
6022           continue;
6023         }
6024 
6025         if (vmIntrinsics::class_for(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id)) == klass_id) {
6026           // Check if the current class contains a method with the same
6027           // name, flags, signature.
6028           bool match = false;
6029           for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6030             const Method* method = methods->at(j);
6031             if (method->intrinsic_id() == id) {
6032               match = true;
6033               break;
6034             }
6035           }
6036 
6037           if (!match) {
6038             char buf[1000];
6039             tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6040                        "but the method is not available in class [%s].%s",
6041                         vmIntrinsics::short_name_as_C_string(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id),
6042                                                              buf, sizeof(buf)),
6043                         ik->name()->as_C_string(),
6044                         NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6045             );
6046             tty->cr();
6047             DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6048           }
6049         }
6050       } // end for
6051     } // CheckIntrinsics
6052 #endif // ASSERT
6053   }
6054 }
6055 
6056 InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::create_instance_klass(bool changed_by_loadhook,
6057                                                       const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6058                                                       TRAPS) {
6059   if (_klass != NULL) {
6060     return _klass;
6061   }
6062 
6063   InstanceKlass* const ik =
6064     InstanceKlass::allocate_instance_klass(*this, CHECK_NULL);
6065 
6066   if (is_hidden()) {
6067     mangle_hidden_class_name(ik);
6068   }
6069 
6070   fill_instance_klass(ik, changed_by_loadhook, cl_inst_info, CHECK_NULL);
6071 
6072   assert(_klass == ik, "invariant");
6073 
6074 
6075   if (ik->should_store_fingerprint()) {
6076     ik->store_fingerprint(_stream->compute_fingerprint());
6077   }
6078 
6079   ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(false);
6080   if (UseAOT && ik->supers_have_passed_fingerprint_checks()) {
6081     uint64_t aot_fp = AOTLoader::get_saved_fingerprint(ik);
6082     uint64_t fp = ik->has_stored_fingerprint() ? ik->get_stored_fingerprint() : _stream->compute_fingerprint();
6083     if (aot_fp != 0 && aot_fp == fp) {
6084       // This class matches with a class saved in an AOT library
6085       ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(true);
6086     } else {
6087       ResourceMark rm;
6088       log_info(class, fingerprint)("%s :  expected = " PTR64_FORMAT " actual = " PTR64_FORMAT,
6089                                  ik->external_name(), aot_fp, _stream->compute_fingerprint());
6090     }
6091   }
6092 
6093   if (ik->is_value()) {
6094     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6095     oop val = ik->allocate_instance(CHECK_NULL);
6096     vk->set_default_value(val);
6097   }
6098 
6099   return ik;
6100 }
6101 
6102 // Return true if the specified class is not a valid super class for an inline type.
6103 // A valid super class for an inline type is abstract, has no instance fields,
6104 // does not implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject (checked elsewhere), has
6105 // an empty body-less no-arg constructor, and no synchronized instance methods.
6106 // This function doesn't check if the class's super types are invalid.  Those checks
6107 // are done elsewhere.  The final determination of whether or not a class is an
6108 // invalid super type for an inline class is done in fill_instance_klass().
6109 bool ClassFileParser::is_invalid_super_for_inline_type() {
6110   if (class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6111     return true;
6112   }
6113   if (is_interface() || class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6114     return false;
6115   }
6116   if (!access_flags().is_abstract() || _has_nonstatic_fields) {
6117     return true;
6118   } else {
6119     // Look at each method
6120     for (int x = 0; x < _methods->length(); x++) {
6121       const Method* const method = _methods->at(x);
6122       if (method->is_synchronized() && !method->is_static()) {
6123         return true;
6124 
6125       } else if (method->name() == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6126         if (method->signature() != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() ||
6127             !method->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
6128           return true;
6129         }
6130       }
6131     }
6132   }
6133   return false;
6134 }
6135 
6136 void ClassFileParser::fill_instance_klass(InstanceKlass* ik,
6137                                           bool changed_by_loadhook,
6138                                           const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6139                                           TRAPS) {
6140   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6141 
6142   // Set name and CLD before adding to CLD
6143   ik->set_class_loader_data(_loader_data);
6144   ik->set_name(_class_name);
6145 
6146   // Add all classes to our internal class loader list here,
6147   // including classes in the bootstrap (NULL) class loader.
6148   const bool publicize = !is_internal();
6149 
6150   _loader_data->add_class(ik, publicize);
6151 
6152   set_klass_to_deallocate(ik);
6153 
6154   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6155   assert(ik->static_field_size() == _field_info->_static_field_size, "sanity");
6156   assert(ik->nonstatic_oop_map_count() == _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count,
6157          "sanity");
6158 
6159   assert(ik->is_instance_klass(), "sanity");
6160   assert(ik->size_helper() == _field_info->_instance_size, "sanity");
6161 
6162   // Fill in information already parsed
6163   ik->set_should_verify_class(_need_verify);
6164 
6165   // Not yet: supers are done below to support the new subtype-checking fields
6166   ik->set_nonstatic_field_size(_field_info->_nonstatic_field_size);
6167   ik->set_has_nonstatic_fields(_field_info->_has_nonstatic_fields);
6168   if (_field_info->_is_naturally_atomic && ik->is_value()) {
6169     ik->set_is_naturally_atomic();
6170   }
6171   if (_is_empty_inline_type) {
6172     ik->set_is_empty_inline_type();
6173   }
6174 
6175   if (this->_invalid_inline_super) {
6176     ik->set_invalid_inline_super();
6177   }
6178 
6179   if (_has_injected_identityObject) {
6180     ik->set_has_injected_identityObject();
6181   }
6182 
6183   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
6184   ik->set_static_oop_field_count(_fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + _fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]);
6185 
6186   // this transfers ownership of a lot of arrays from
6187   // the parser onto the InstanceKlass*
6188   apply_parsed_class_metadata(ik, _java_fields_count, CHECK);
6189 
6190   // can only set dynamic nest-host after static nest information is set
6191   if (cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host() != NULL) {
6192     ik->set_nest_host(cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host(), THREAD);
6193   }
6194 
6195   // note that is not safe to use the fields in the parser from this point on
6196   assert(NULL == _cp, "invariant");
6197   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
6198   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
6199   assert(NULL == _inner_classes, "invariant");
6200   assert(NULL == _nest_members, "invariant");
6201   assert(NULL == _local_interfaces, "invariant");
6202   assert(NULL == _combined_annotations, "invariant");
6203   assert(NULL == _record_components, "invariant");
6204 
6205   if (_has_final_method) {
6206     ik->set_has_final_method();
6207   }
6208 
6209   ik->copy_method_ordering(_method_ordering, CHECK);
6210   // The InstanceKlass::_methods_jmethod_ids cache
6211   // is managed on the assumption that the initial cache
6212   // size is equal to the number of methods in the class. If
6213   // that changes, then InstanceKlass::idnum_can_increment()
6214   // has to be changed accordingly.
6215   ik->set_initial_method_idnum(ik->methods()->length());
6216 
6217   ik->set_this_class_index(_this_class_index);
6218 
6219   if (_is_hidden || is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
6220     // _this_class_index is a CONSTANT_Class entry that refers to this
6221     // hidden or anonymous class itself. If this class needs to refer to its own
6222     // methods or fields, it would use a CONSTANT_MethodRef, etc, which would reference
6223     // _this_class_index. However, because this class is hidden or anonymous (it's
6224     // not stored in SystemDictionary), _this_class_index cannot be resolved
6225     // with ConstantPool::klass_at_impl, which does a SystemDictionary lookup.
6226     // Therefore, we must eagerly resolve _this_class_index now.
6227     ik->constants()->klass_at_put(_this_class_index, ik);
6228   }
6229 
6230   ik->set_minor_version(_minor_version);
6231   ik->set_major_version(_major_version);
6232   ik->set_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6233   ik->set_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6234   if (_is_declared_atomic) {
6235     ik->set_is_declared_atomic();
6236   }
6237 
6238   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6239     assert (ik->is_unsafe_anonymous(), "should be the same");
6240     ik->set_unsafe_anonymous_host(_unsafe_anonymous_host);
6241   }
6242   if (_is_hidden) {
6243     ik->set_is_hidden();
6244   }
6245 
6246   // Set PackageEntry for this_klass
6247   oop cl = ik->class_loader();
6248   Handle clh = Handle(THREAD, java_lang_ClassLoader::non_reflection_class_loader(cl));
6249   ClassLoaderData* cld = ClassLoaderData::class_loader_data_or_null(clh());
6250   ik->set_package(cld, NULL, CHECK);
6251 
6252   const Array<Method*>* const methods = ik->methods();
6253   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6254   const int methods_len = methods->length();
6255 
6256   check_methods_for_intrinsics(ik, methods);
6257 
6258   // Fill in field values obtained by parse_classfile_attributes
6259   if (_parsed_annotations->has_any_annotations()) {
6260     _parsed_annotations->apply_to(ik);
6261   }
6262 
6263   apply_parsed_class_attributes(ik);
6264 
6265   // Miranda methods
6266   if ((_num_miranda_methods > 0) ||
6267       // if this class introduced new miranda methods or
6268       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_miranda_methods())
6269         // super class exists and this class inherited miranda methods
6270      ) {
6271        ik->set_has_miranda_methods(); // then set a flag
6272   }
6273 
6274   // Fill in information needed to compute superclasses.
6275   ik->initialize_supers(const_cast<InstanceKlass*>(_super_klass), _transitive_interfaces, CHECK);
6276   ik->set_transitive_interfaces(_transitive_interfaces);
6277   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6278 
6279   // Initialize itable offset tables
6280   klassItable::setup_itable_offset_table(ik);
6281 
6282   // Compute transitive closure of interfaces this class implements
6283   // Do final class setup
6284   OopMapBlocksBuilder* oop_map_blocks = _field_info->oop_map_blocks;
6285   if (oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
6286     oop_map_blocks->copy(ik->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps());
6287   }
6288 
6289   if (_has_contended_fields || _parsed_annotations->is_contended() ||
6290       ( _super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_contended_annotations())) {
6291     ik->set_has_contended_annotations(true);
6292   }
6293 
6294   // Fill in has_finalizer, has_vanilla_constructor, and layout_helper
6295   set_precomputed_flags(ik);
6296 
6297   // check if this class can access its super class
6298   check_super_class_access(ik, CHECK);
6299 
6300   // check if this class can access its superinterfaces
6301   check_super_interface_access(ik, CHECK);
6302 
6303   // check if this class overrides any final method
6304   check_final_method_override(ik, CHECK);
6305 
6306   // reject static interface methods prior to Java 8
6307   if (ik->is_interface() && _major_version < JAVA_8_VERSION) {
6308     check_illegal_static_method(ik, CHECK);
6309   }
6310 
6311   // Obtain this_klass' module entry
6312   ModuleEntry* module_entry = ik->module();
6313   assert(module_entry != NULL, "module_entry should always be set");
6314 
6315   // Obtain java.lang.Module
6316   Handle module_handle(THREAD, module_entry->module());
6317 
6318   // Allocate mirror and initialize static fields
6319   // The create_mirror() call will also call compute_modifiers()
6320   java_lang_Class::create_mirror(ik,
6321                                  Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
6322                                  module_handle,
6323                                  _protection_domain,
6324                                  cl_inst_info.class_data(),
6325                                  CHECK);
6326 
6327   assert(_all_mirandas != NULL, "invariant");
6328 
6329   // Generate any default methods - default methods are public interface methods
6330   // that have a default implementation.  This is new with Java 8.
6331   if (_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6332     DefaultMethods::generate_default_methods(ik,
6333                                              _all_mirandas,
6334                                              CHECK);
6335   }
6336 
6337   // Add read edges to the unnamed modules of the bootstrap and app class loaders.
6338   if (changed_by_loadhook && !module_handle.is_null() && module_entry->is_named() &&
6339       !module_entry->has_default_read_edges()) {
6340     if (!module_entry->set_has_default_read_edges()) {
6341       // We won a potential race
6342       JvmtiExport::add_default_read_edges(module_handle, THREAD);
6343     }
6344   }
6345 
6346   int nfields = ik->java_fields_count();
6347   if (ik->is_value()) nfields++;
6348   for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {
6349     if (ik->field_is_flattenable(i)) {
6350       Symbol* klass_name = ik->field_signature(i)->fundamental_name(CHECK);
6351       // Inline classes for instance fields must have been pre-loaded
6352       // Inline classes for static fields might not have been loaded yet
6353       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::find(klass_name,
6354           Handle(THREAD, ik->class_loader()),
6355           Handle(THREAD, ik->protection_domain()), CHECK);
6356       if (klass != NULL) {
6357         assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
6358         ik->set_value_field_klass(i, klass);
6359       }
6360       klass_name->decrement_refcount();
6361     } else
6362       if (is_inline_type() && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL) != 0)
6363         && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) != 0)) {
6364       ValueKlass::cast(ik)->set_default_value_offset(ik->field_offset(i));
6365     }
6366   }
6367 
6368   if (is_inline_type()) {
6369     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6370     if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
6371       vk->set_alignment(_alignment);
6372       vk->set_first_field_offset(_first_field_offset);
6373       vk->set_exact_size_in_bytes(_exact_size_in_bytes);
6374     } else {
6375       vk->set_first_field_offset(vk->first_field_offset_old());
6376     }
6377     ValueKlass::cast(ik)->initialize_calling_convention(CHECK);
6378   }
6379 
6380   ClassLoadingService::notify_class_loaded(ik, false /* not shared class */);
6381 
6382   if (!is_internal()) {
6383     if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, load)) {
6384       ResourceMark rm;
6385       const char* module_name = (module_entry->name() == NULL) ? UNNAMED_MODULE : module_entry->name()->as_C_string();
6386       ik->print_class_load_logging(_loader_data, module_name, _stream);
6387     }
6388 
6389     if (ik->minor_version() == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
6390         ik->major_version() == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
6391         log_is_enabled(Info, class, preview)) {
6392       ResourceMark rm;
6393       log_info(class, preview)("Loading class %s that depends on preview features (class file version %d.65535)",
6394                                ik->external_name(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
6395     }
6396 
6397     if (log_is_enabled(Debug, class, resolve))  {
6398       ResourceMark rm;
6399       // print out the superclass.
6400       const char * from = ik->external_name();
6401       if (ik->java_super() != NULL) {
6402         log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (super)",
6403                    from,
6404                    ik->java_super()->external_name());
6405       }
6406       // print out each of the interface classes referred to by this class.
6407       const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = ik->local_interfaces();
6408       if (local_interfaces != NULL) {
6409         const int length = local_interfaces->length();
6410         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
6411           const InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
6412           const char * to = k->external_name();
6413           log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (interface)", from, to);
6414         }
6415       }
6416     }
6417   }
6418 
6419   JFR_ONLY(INIT_ID(ik);)
6420 
6421   // If we reach here, all is well.
6422   // Now remove the InstanceKlass* from the _klass_to_deallocate field
6423   // in order for it to not be destroyed in the ClassFileParser destructor.
6424   set_klass_to_deallocate(NULL);
6425 
6426   // it's official
6427   set_klass(ik);
6428 
6429   if (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6430     Universe::initialize_the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array(ik, CHECK);
6431   }
6432 
6433   debug_only(ik->verify();)
6434 }
6435 
6436 void ClassFileParser::update_class_name(Symbol* new_class_name) {
6437   // Decrement the refcount in the old name, since we're clobbering it.
6438   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6439 
6440   _class_name = new_class_name;
6441   // Increment the refcount of the new name.
6442   // Now the ClassFileParser owns this name and will decrement in
6443   // the destructor.
6444   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6445 }
6446 
6447 // For an unsafe anonymous class that is in the unnamed package, move it to its host class's
6448 // package by prepending its host class's package name to its class name and setting
6449 // its _class_name field.
6450 void ClassFileParser::prepend_host_package_name(const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host, TRAPS) {
6451   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6452   assert(strrchr(_class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) == NULL,
6453          "Unsafe anonymous class should not be in a package");
6454   TempNewSymbol host_pkg_name =
6455     ClassLoader::package_from_class_name(unsafe_anonymous_host->name());
6456 
6457   if (host_pkg_name != NULL) {
6458     int host_pkg_len = host_pkg_name->utf8_length();
6459     int class_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length();
6460     int symbol_len = host_pkg_len + 1 + class_name_len;
6461     char* new_anon_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, symbol_len + 1);
6462     int n = os::snprintf(new_anon_name, symbol_len + 1, "%.*s/%.*s",
6463                          host_pkg_len, host_pkg_name->base(), class_name_len, _class_name->base());
6464     assert(n == symbol_len, "Unexpected number of characters in string");
6465 
6466     // Decrement old _class_name to avoid leaking.
6467     _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6468 
6469     // Create a symbol and update the anonymous class name.
6470     // The new class name is created with a refcount of one. When installed into the InstanceKlass,
6471     // it'll be two and when the ClassFileParser destructor runs, it'll go back to one and get deleted
6472     // when the class is unloaded.
6473     _class_name = SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_anon_name, symbol_len);
6474   }
6475 }
6476 
6477 // If the host class and the anonymous class are in the same package then do
6478 // nothing.  If the anonymous class is in the unnamed package then move it to its
6479 // host's package.  If the classes are in different packages then throw an IAE
6480 // exception.
6481 void ClassFileParser::fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(TRAPS) {
6482   assert(_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL, "Expected an unsafe anonymous class");
6483 
6484   const jbyte* anon_last_slash = UTF8::strrchr((const jbyte*)_class_name->base(),
6485                                                _class_name->utf8_length(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH);
6486   if (anon_last_slash == NULL) {  // Unnamed package
6487     prepend_host_package_name(_unsafe_anonymous_host, CHECK);
6488   } else {
6489     if (!_unsafe_anonymous_host->is_same_class_package(_unsafe_anonymous_host->class_loader(), _class_name)) {
6490       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6491       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(),
6492         err_msg("Host class %s and anonymous class %s are in different packages",
6493         _unsafe_anonymous_host->name()->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string()));
6494     }
6495   }
6496 }
6497 
6498 static bool relax_format_check_for(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) {
6499   bool trusted = loader_data->is_boot_class_loader_data() ||
6500                  loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data();
6501   bool need_verify =
6502     // verifyAll
6503     (BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote) ||
6504     // verifyRemote
6505     (!BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote && !trusted);
6506   return !need_verify;
6507 }
6508 
6509 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6510                                  Symbol* name,
6511                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6512                                  const ClassLoadInfo* cl_info,
6513                                  Publicity pub_level,
6514                                  TRAPS) :
6515   _stream(stream),
6516   _class_name(NULL),
6517   _loader_data(loader_data),
6518   _unsafe_anonymous_host(cl_info->unsafe_anonymous_host()),
6519   _cp_patches(cl_info->cp_patches()),
6520   _is_hidden(cl_info->is_hidden()),
6521   _can_access_vm_annotations(cl_info->can_access_vm_annotations()),
6522   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6523   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6524   _orig_cp_size(0),
6525   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6526   _super_klass(),
6527   _cp(NULL),
6528   _fields(NULL),
6529   _methods(NULL),
6530   _inner_classes(NULL),
6531   _nest_members(NULL),
6532   _nest_host(0),
6533   _record_components(NULL),
6534   _temp_local_interfaces(NULL),
6535   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6536   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6537   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6538   _class_annotations(NULL),
6539   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6540   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6541   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6542   _klass(NULL),
6543   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6544   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6545   _fac(NULL),
6546   _field_info(NULL),
6547   _method_ordering(NULL),
6548   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6549   _vtable_size(0),
6550   _itable_size(0),
6551   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6552   _rt(REF_NONE),
6553   _protection_domain(cl_info->protection_domain()),
6554   _access_flags(),
6555   _pub_level(pub_level),
6556   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6557   _synthetic_flag(false),
6558   _sde_length(false),
6559   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6560   _sourcefile_index(0),
6561   _generic_signature_index(0),
6562   _major_version(0),
6563   _minor_version(0),
6564   _this_class_index(0),
6565   _super_class_index(0),
6566   _itfs_len(0),
6567   _java_fields_count(0),
6568   _need_verify(false),
6569   _relax_verify(false),
6570   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6571   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6572   _has_final_method(false),
6573   _has_contended_fields(false),
6574   _has_flattenable_fields(false),
6575   _has_nonstatic_fields(false),
6576   _is_empty_inline_type(false),
6577   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6578   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6579   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6580   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6581   _implements_identityObject(false),
6582   _has_injected_identityObject(false),
6583   _has_finalizer(false),
6584   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6585   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6586   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6587 
6588   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6589   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6590 
6591   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6592   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6593   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6594   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6595   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6596   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6597   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6598 
6599   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6600   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6601     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6602     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6603     // for those classes.
6604     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6605                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6606   }
6607   else {
6608     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6609                                                stream->need_verify());
6610   }
6611   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6612     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6613     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6614       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6615         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6616         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6617           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6618           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6619           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6620           // calls patch_class().
6621           //
6622           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6623           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6624           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6625           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6626         }
6627       }
6628     }
6629   }
6630 
6631   // synch back verification state to stream
6632   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6633 
6634   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6635   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6636   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6637 
6638   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6639 
6640   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6641 }
6642 
6643 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6644   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6645   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6646   _cp = NULL;
6647   _fields = NULL;
6648   _methods = NULL;
6649   _inner_classes = NULL;
6650   _nest_members = NULL;
6651   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6652   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6653   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6654   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6655   _record_components = NULL;
6656 }
6657 
6658 // Destructor to clean up
6659 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6660   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6661 
6662   if (_cp != NULL) {
6663     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6664   }
6665   if (_fields != NULL) {
6666     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6667   }
6668 
6669   if (_methods != NULL) {
6670     // Free methods
6671     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6672   }
6673 
6674   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6675   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6676     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6677   }
6678 
6679   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6680     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6681   }
6682 
6683   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6684     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6685   }
6686 
6687   // Free interfaces
6688   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6689                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6690 
6691   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6692     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6693     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6694 
6695     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6696     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6697 
6698     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6699     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6700     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6701     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6702     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6703     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6704   } else {
6705     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6706     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6707     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6708     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6709     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6710     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6711   }
6712 
6713   clear_class_metadata();
6714   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6715 
6716   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6717   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6718   // at a safepoint.
6719   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6720     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6721   }
6722 }
6723 
6724 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6725                                    TRAPS) {
6726 
6727   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6728   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6729 
6730   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6731   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6732   // Magic value
6733   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6734   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6735                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6736                      magic, CHECK);
6737 
6738   // Version numbers
6739   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6740   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6741 
6742   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6743     ResourceMark rm;
6744     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6745             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6746     Exceptions::fthrow(
6747       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6748       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6749       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6750       _major_version,
6751       _minor_version);
6752   }
6753 
6754   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6755   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6756 
6757   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6758   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6759 
6760   guarantee_property(
6761     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6762     cp_size, CHECK);
6763 
6764   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6765   if (is_hidden()) { // Add a slot for hidden class name.
6766     assert(_max_num_patched_klasses == 0, "Sanity check");
6767     cp_size++;
6768   } else {
6769     if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6770       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6771     }
6772     cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6773   }
6774 
6775   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6776                                cp_size,
6777                                CHECK);
6778 
6779   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6780 
6781   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6782 
6783   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6784 
6785   // ACCESS FLAGS
6786   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6787 
6788   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6789   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6790   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6791     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6792   }
6793   // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6794   if (supports_inline_types()) {
6795     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
6796   }
6797 
6798   // Access flags
6799   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6800 
6801   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6802     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6803     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6804   }
6805 
6806   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6807 
6808   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6809   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6810     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6811     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6812     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6813   }
6814 
6815   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6816 
6817   // This class and superclass
6818   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6819   check_property(
6820     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6821       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6822     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6823     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6824 
6825   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6826   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6827 
6828   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6829   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6830   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6831   if (_need_verify) {
6832     guarantee_property(class_name_in_cp->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6833                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6834                        CHECK);
6835   }
6836 
6837 #ifdef ASSERT
6838   // Basic sanity checks
6839   assert(!(_is_hidden && (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL)), "mutually exclusive variants");
6840 
6841   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6842     assert(_class_name == vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "A named anonymous class???");
6843   }
6844   if (_is_hidden) {
6845     assert(_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "hidden classes should have a special name");
6846   }
6847 #endif
6848 
6849   // Update the _class_name as needed depending on whether this is a named,
6850   // un-named, hidden or unsafe-anonymous class.
6851 
6852   if (_is_hidden) {
6853     assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
6854 #ifdef ASSERT
6855     if (_need_verify) {
6856       verify_legal_class_name(_class_name, CHECK);
6857     }
6858 #endif
6859 
6860   // NOTE: !_is_hidden does not imply "findable" as it could be an old-style
6861   //       "hidden" unsafe-anonymous class
6862 
6863   // If this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it is in the unnamed
6864   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6865   // its host class.
6866   } else if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6867     update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6868     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6869 
6870   } else {
6871     // Check if name in class file matches given name
6872     if (_class_name != class_name_in_cp) {
6873       if (_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name()) {
6874         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6875         Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6876                            vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
6877                            "%s (wrong name: %s)",
6878                            class_name_in_cp->as_C_string(),
6879                            _class_name->as_C_string()
6880                            );
6881         return;
6882       } else {
6883         // The class name was not known by the caller so we set it from
6884         // the value in the CP.
6885         update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6886       }
6887       // else nothing to do: the expected class name matches what is in the CP
6888     }
6889   }
6890 
6891   // Verification prevents us from creating names with dots in them, this
6892   // asserts that that's the case.
6893   assert(is_internal_format(_class_name), "external class name format used internally");
6894 
6895   if (!is_internal()) {
6896     LogTarget(Debug, class, preorder) lt;
6897     if (lt.is_enabled()){
6898       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6899       LogStream ls(lt);
6900       ls.print("%s", _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
6901       if (stream->source() != NULL) {
6902         ls.print(" source: %s", stream->source());
6903       }
6904       ls.cr();
6905     }
6906 
6907 #if INCLUDE_CDS
6908     if (DumpLoadedClassList != NULL && stream->source() != NULL && classlist_file->is_open()) {
6909       if (!ClassLoader::has_jrt_entry()) {
6910         warning("DumpLoadedClassList and CDS are not supported in exploded build");
6911         DumpLoadedClassList = NULL;
6912       } else if (SystemDictionaryShared::is_sharing_possible(_loader_data) &&
6913                  !_is_hidden &&
6914                  _unsafe_anonymous_host == NULL) {
6915         // Only dump the classes that can be stored into CDS archive.
6916         // Hidden and unsafe anonymous classes such as generated LambdaForm classes are also not included.
6917         oop class_loader = _loader_data->class_loader();
6918         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6919         bool skip = false;
6920         if (class_loader == NULL || SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(class_loader)) {
6921           // For the boot and platform class loaders, skip classes that are not found in the
6922           // java runtime image, such as those found in the --patch-module entries.
6923           // These classes can't be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6924           if (!stream->from_boot_loader_modules_image() && strncmp(stream->source(), "jrt:", 4) != 0) {
6925             skip = true;
6926           }
6927 
6928           if (class_loader == NULL && ClassLoader::contains_append_entry(stream->source())) {
6929             // .. but don't skip the boot classes that are loaded from -Xbootclasspath/a
6930             // as they can be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6931             skip = false;
6932           }
6933         }
6934         if (skip) {
6935           tty->print_cr("skip writing class %s from source %s to classlist file",
6936             _class_name->as_C_string(), stream->source());
6937         } else {
6938           classlist_file->print_cr("%s", _class_name->as_C_string());
6939           classlist_file->flush();
6940         }
6941       }
6942     }
6943 #endif
6944   }
6945 
6946   // SUPERKLASS
6947   _super_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6948   _super_klass = parse_super_class(cp,
6949                                    _super_class_index,
6950                                    _need_verify,
6951                                    CHECK);
6952 
6953   // Interfaces
6954   _itfs_len = stream->get_u2_fast();
6955   parse_interfaces(stream,
6956                    _itfs_len,
6957                    cp,
6958                    is_inline_type(),
6959                    &_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6960                    &_is_declared_atomic,
6961                    CHECK);
6962 
6963   assert(_temp_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
6964 
6965   // Fields (offsets are filled in later)
6966   _fac = new FieldAllocationCount();
6967   parse_fields(stream,
6968                is_interface(),
6969                is_inline_type(),
6970                _fac,
6971                cp,
6972                cp_size,
6973                &_java_fields_count,
6974                CHECK);
6975 
6976   assert(_fields != NULL, "invariant");
6977 
6978   // Methods
6979   AccessFlags promoted_flags;
6980   parse_methods(stream,
6981                 is_interface(),
6982                 is_inline_type(),
6983                 &promoted_flags,
6984                 &_has_final_method,
6985                 &_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6986                 CHECK);
6987 
6988   assert(_methods != NULL, "invariant");
6989 
6990   // promote flags from parse_methods() to the klass' flags
6991   _access_flags.add_promoted_flags(promoted_flags.as_int());
6992 
6993   if (_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6994     _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6995   }
6996 
6997   // Additional attributes/annotations
6998   _parsed_annotations = new ClassAnnotationCollector();
6999   parse_classfile_attributes(stream, cp, _parsed_annotations, CHECK);
7000 
7001   assert(_inner_classes != NULL, "invariant");
7002 
7003   // Finalize the Annotations metadata object,
7004   // now that all annotation arrays have been created.
7005   create_combined_annotations(CHECK);
7006 
7007   // Make sure this is the end of class file stream
7008   guarantee_property(stream->at_eos(),
7009                      "Extra bytes at the end of class file %s",
7010                      CHECK);
7011 
7012   // all bytes in stream read and parsed
7013 }
7014 
7015 void ClassFileParser::mangle_hidden_class_name(InstanceKlass* const ik) {
7016   ResourceMark rm;
7017   // Construct hidden name from _class_name, "+", and &ik. Note that we can't
7018   // use a '/' because that confuses finding the class's package.  Also, can't
7019   // use an illegal char such as ';' because that causes serialization issues
7020   // and issues with hidden classes that create their own hidden classes.
7021   char addr_buf[20];
7022   jio_snprintf(addr_buf, 20, INTPTR_FORMAT, p2i(ik));
7023   size_t new_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length() + 2 + strlen(addr_buf);
7024   char* new_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, new_name_len);
7025   jio_snprintf(new_name, new_name_len, "%s+%s",
7026                _class_name->as_C_string(), addr_buf);
7027   update_class_name(SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_name));
7028 
7029   // Add a Utf8 entry containing the hidden name.
7030   assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
7031   int hidden_index = _orig_cp_size; // this is an extra slot we added
7032   _cp->symbol_at_put(hidden_index, _class_name);
7033 
7034   // Update this_class_index's slot in the constant pool with the new Utf8 entry.
7035   // We have to update the resolved_klass_index and the name_index together
7036   // so extract the existing resolved_klass_index first.
7037   CPKlassSlot cp_klass_slot = _cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index);
7038   int resolved_klass_index = cp_klass_slot.resolved_klass_index();
7039   _cp->unresolved_klass_at_put(_this_class_index, hidden_index, resolved_klass_index);
7040   assert(_cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index).name_index() == _orig_cp_size,
7041          "Bad name_index");
7042 }
7043 
7044 void ClassFileParser::post_process_parsed_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
7045                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
7046                                                  TRAPS) {
7047   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
7048   assert(stream->at_eos(), "invariant");
7049   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
7050   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
7051 
7052   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
7053     check_property(_temp_local_interfaces->length() == 0,
7054         "java.lang.Object cannot implement an interface in class file %s",
7055         CHECK);
7056   }
7057   // We check super class after class file is parsed and format is checked
7058   if (_super_class_index > 0 && NULL ==_super_klass) {
7059     Symbol* const super_class_name = cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index);
7060     if (is_interface()) {
7061       // Before attempting to resolve the superclass, check for class format
7062       // errors not checked yet.
7063       guarantee_property(super_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object(),
7064         "Interfaces must have java.lang.Object as superclass in class file %s",
7065         CHECK);
7066     }
7067     Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7068     _super_klass = (const InstanceKlass*)
7069                        SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(_class_name,
7070                                                                super_class_name,
7071                                                                loader,
7072                                                                _protection_domain,
7073                                                                true,
7074                                                                CHECK);
7075   }
7076 
7077   if (_super_klass != NULL) {
7078     if (_super_klass->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
7079       _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
7080     }
7081     if (_super_klass->is_declared_atomic()) {
7082       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7083     }
7084 
7085     if (_super_klass->is_interface()) {
7086       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7087       Exceptions::fthrow(
7088         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7089         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7090         "class %s has interface %s as super class",
7091         _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7092         _super_klass->external_name()
7093       );
7094       return;
7095     }
7096 
7097     // Make sure super class is not final
7098     if (_super_klass->is_final()) {
7099       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(), "Cannot inherit from final class");
7100     }
7101 
7102     // For an inline class, only java/lang/Object or special abstract classes
7103     // are acceptable super classes.
7104     if (is_inline_type()) {
7105       const InstanceKlass* super_ik = _super_klass;
7106       if (super_ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
7107         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7108         Exceptions::fthrow(
7109           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7110           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7111           "inline class %s has an invalid super class %s",
7112           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7113           _super_klass->external_name());
7114         return;
7115       }
7116     }
7117   }
7118 
7119   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_NonTearable() && _loader_data->class_loader() == NULL) {
7120     // This is the original source of this condition.
7121     // It propagates by inheritance, as if testing "instanceof NonTearable".
7122     _is_declared_atomic = true;
7123   } else if (*ForceNonTearable != '\0') {
7124     // Allow a command line switch to force the same atomicity property:
7125     const char* class_name_str = _class_name->as_C_string();
7126     if (StringUtils::class_list_match(ForceNonTearable, class_name_str)) {
7127       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7128     }
7129   }
7130 
7131   // Set ik->invalid_inline_super field to TRUE if already marked as invalid,
7132   // if super is marked invalid, or if is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()
7133   // returns true
7134   if (invalid_inline_super() ||
7135       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->invalid_inline_super()) ||
7136       is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()) {
7137     set_invalid_inline_super();
7138   }
7139 
7140   if (!is_inline_type() && invalid_inline_super() && (_super_klass == NULL || !_super_klass->invalid_inline_super())
7141       && !_implements_identityObject && class_name() != vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
7142     _temp_local_interfaces->append(SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass());
7143     _has_injected_identityObject = true;
7144   }
7145   int itfs_len = _temp_local_interfaces->length();
7146   if (itfs_len == 0) {
7147     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
7148   } else if (itfs_len == 1 && _temp_local_interfaces->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
7149     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
7150   } else {
7151     _local_interfaces = MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(_loader_data, itfs_len, NULL, CHECK);
7152     for (int i = 0; i < itfs_len; i++) {
7153       _local_interfaces->at_put(i, _temp_local_interfaces->at(i));
7154     }
7155   }
7156   _temp_local_interfaces = NULL;
7157   assert(_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7158 
7159   // Compute the transitive list of all unique interfaces implemented by this class
7160   _transitive_interfaces =
7161     compute_transitive_interfaces(_super_klass,
7162                                   _local_interfaces,
7163                                   _loader_data,
7164                                   CHECK);
7165 
7166   assert(_transitive_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7167 
7168   // sort methods
7169   _method_ordering = sort_methods(_methods);
7170 
7171   _all_mirandas = new GrowableArray<Method*>(20);
7172 
7173   Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7174   klassVtable::compute_vtable_size_and_num_mirandas(&_vtable_size,
7175                                                     &_num_miranda_methods,
7176                                                     _all_mirandas,
7177                                                     _super_klass,
7178                                                     _methods,
7179                                                     _access_flags,
7180                                                     _major_version,
7181                                                     loader,
7182                                                     _class_name,
7183                                                     _local_interfaces,
7184                                                     CHECK);
7185 
7186   // Size of Java itable (in words)
7187   _itable_size = is_interface() ? 0 :
7188     klassItable::compute_itable_size(_transitive_interfaces);
7189 
7190   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
7191   assert(_parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
7192 
7193 
7194   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
7195     if (fs.is_flattenable() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
7196       // Pre-load value class
7197       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
7198           Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
7199           _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
7200       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
7201       assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
7202       _has_flattenable_fields = true;
7203     }
7204   }
7205 
7206   _field_info = new FieldLayoutInfo();
7207   if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
7208     FieldLayoutBuilder lb(class_name(), super_klass(), _cp, _fields,
7209         _parsed_annotations->is_contended(), is_inline_type(),
7210         loader_data(), _protection_domain, _field_info);
7211     lb.build_layout(CHECK);
7212     if (is_inline_type()) {
7213       _alignment = lb.get_alignment();
7214       _first_field_offset = lb.get_first_field_offset();
7215       _exact_size_in_bytes = lb.get_exact_size_in_byte();
7216     }
7217   } else {
7218     layout_fields(cp, _fac, _parsed_annotations, _field_info, CHECK);
7219   }
7220 
7221   // Compute reference type
7222   _rt = (NULL ==_super_klass) ? REF_NONE : _super_klass->reference_type();
7223 }
7224 
7225 void ClassFileParser::set_klass(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7226 
7227 #ifdef ASSERT
7228   if (klass != NULL) {
7229     assert(NULL == _klass, "leaking?");
7230   }
7231 #endif
7232 
7233   _klass = klass;
7234 }
7235 
7236 void ClassFileParser::set_klass_to_deallocate(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7237 
7238 #ifdef ASSERT
7239   if (klass != NULL) {
7240     assert(NULL == _klass_to_deallocate, "leaking?");
7241   }
7242 #endif
7243 
7244   _klass_to_deallocate = klass;
7245 }
7246 
7247 // Caller responsible for ResourceMark
7248 // clone stream with rewound position
7249 const ClassFileStream* ClassFileParser::clone_stream() const {
7250   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
7251 
7252   return _stream->clone();
7253 }

7255 // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
7256 // debugging
7257 
7258 #ifdef ASSERT
7259 
7260 // return true if class_name contains no '.' (internal format is '/')
7261 bool ClassFileParser::is_internal_format(Symbol* class_name) {
7262   if (class_name != NULL) {
7263     ResourceMark rm;
7264     char* name = class_name->as_C_string();
7265     return strchr(name, JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT) == NULL;
7266   } else {
7267     return true;
7268   }
7269 }
7270 
7271 #endif
